 Reliance Jio's 3-month preview offer is available for almost all 4G smartphones
 aise main reliance digital par lambii line laganaa aam baat ho gai he
 In view of all this, many telecom companies have also started offering offers
 bharti airetail ne do nae data plance kaa elaan kiya he
 It is being called Mega Saver Pack which will be valid for all prepaid customers across the country
 company ne 1,498 or 748 rupee kaa do 4G / 3G plan shuru kiya he
 It will have a validity of 28 days and after the data limit is over, users will have to recharge Rs 51 for 1GB 4G / 3G data
 khaas baat yah he ki aisa ek saal tak ke liye hoga
 That is, you will be charged 51 rupees every month for 1GB of data
 iske alaava 99 rupee ke top ap par 2GB data milegaa
 You will get 28 days validity on every recharge
 is plan kii khaasiyat yah he ki ek saal ke dauraan aap kai baar richarge kara ke data hasil kar sakate hai
 There is no limit for this
 philhal ise dilli-ensiaar ke liye shuru kiya gaya he or jald hi yah desh bhar main uplabdh hoga
 Significantly, if you take 1GB 3G / 4G data for a month, then for this you are charged Rs 259
 aise main is plan ke liye ek baar aapako zyada paisa lagaana hoga, lekin ek saal tak ke liye aapako phayda hoga

 Today is the birthday of Mohammed Rafi, the uncrowned king of Hindi cinema
 aaj bhi rafee sahab ke gane kaaphi lokapriy hai
 a funk that people still remember through his songs
 search ingine google ne bhi rafee sahab par doodle banaakar unhen shradhanjali di he
 Apart from Hindi, Mohammed Rafi has sung songs in Assamese, Konkani, Bhojpuri, Odia, Punjabi, Bengali, Marathi, Sindhi, Kannada, Gujarati, Telugu, Maghi, Maithili, Urdu, as well as English, Persian, Arabic and Dutch languages
 , Let's know some special things about Mohammed Rafi Sahab
 
 
 - mohammad rafee kaa janm 24 disambar 1924 ko amritsar (punjab) main hua tha
 After a time Rafi Saheb's father moved to Lahore with his family
 - mohammad rafee kaa nik nem 'fico' tha or bachapan se hi raah chalate fakiron ko sunate hue rafee sahab ne gaanaa shuru kar diya tha
 - Mohammad Rafi studied classical music from Ustad Abdul Wahid Khan, Pandit Jeevan Lal Mattoo and Feroz Nizami
 saat suron ke sabase bade fankaar mohammad rafee kaa aaj janmdin he
 
 
 - At the age of 13, Mohammed Rafi gave public performance in Lahore by singing songs of the then famous actor 'KL El Saigal'
 - rafee sahab ne sabase pehle lahore main punjabi film 'gul baloch' ke liye 'goriye ni, hiriye ni' gaanaa gaaya tha
 - Mohammad Rafi came to Mumbai and sang the song for the Hindi film for the first time in 1944
 film kaa naam 'gaanv kii gori' tha
 - Mohammed Rafi was considered a compassionate singer, as he never mentioned the fees for the song and sometimes even sang the song for 1 rupee
 mohammad rafee ke janmdin par sunen unke behtareen gane- mohammad rafee ne sabase zyada duat gane 'aashaa bhosle' ke saath gaae hai
 Rafi Saab also voiced for singer Kishore Kumar in his two films 'bade Sarkar' and 'ragini'
